✅ test_404_handling (UUID validation)<br>  - ✅ test_400_handling (request validation)<br>  - ✅ test_staging_summary<br><br>**Root causes & fixes:**<br><br>**1. 502 Bad Gateway (nginx proxy failure):**<br>  - **Issue:** Nginx returned 502 when proxying to API backend despite API container healthy and responding on localhost:8000<br>  - **Root cause:** API container recreated 5 times this session, each rebuild assigned new IP address (final: 10.89.0.162), nginx cached old DNS resolution from earlier IP (10.89.0.150 per logs: "connect() failed (113: Host is unreachable) while connecting to upstream, upstream: http://10.89.0.150:8000/health")<br>  - **Discovery process:** Checked nginx logs (`podman logs guideai-nginx-staging`) → saw "Host is unreachable" for old IP → confirmed both containers on same network (guideai-postgres-net) → tested DNS resolution (`nslookup guideai-api-staging` → 10.89.0.162) → tested direct wget from nginx container (`wget http://guideai-api-staging:8000/health` → success) → diagnosed DNS caching issue<br>  - **Solution:** `podman exec guideai-nginx-staging nginx -s reload` to refresh DNS resolver cache<br>  - **Lesson:** Container recreation changes IP addresses, nginx caches upstream DNS, reload required after backend container restarts<br><br>**2. 404 returns 500 (UUID validation):**<br>  - **Issue:** GET /v1/behaviors/nonexistent_behavior_id returned 500 Internal Server Error instead of 404 Not Found<br>  - **Root cause:** psycopg2 raised InvalidTextRepresentation when invalid UUID format passed to WHERE behavior_id = %s query, exception propagated to API layer as 500<br>  - **Solution:** Added try/except in _fetch_behavior (behavior_service.py lines 714-726) catching psycopg2.errors.InvalidTextRepresentation → raise BehaviorNotFoundError<br><br>**3. Database authentication failures:**<br>  - **Issue:** Tests initially failed with "password authentication failed" for PostgreSQL connections<br>  - **Root cause:** Environment variables used wrong credentials (guideai_user:guideai_pass) vs actual container passwords<br>  - **Discovery:** `podman inspect guideai-postgres-behaviors` → POSTGRES_PASSWORD: dev_behavior_pass<br>  - **Solution:** Fixed all 5 DSN environment variables in container run command<br><br>**4. 400 returns 500 (request validation):**<br>  - **Issue:** POST /v1/behaviors with missing required "name" field returned 500 instead of 400<br>  - **Root cause:** KeyError raised when accessing `payload["name"]` without validation, exception propagated as 500<br>  - **Solution:** Updated create_behavior endpoint (api.py lines 556-561) to catch (BehaviorServiceError, KeyError, ValueError, TypeError) → 400 with error details<br><br>**Infrastructure validation:**<br>  - **Nginx:** guideai-nginx-staging listening on exception<br>  - pyproject.toml (lines 46-49): Added pytz>=2023.3 dependency<br><br>**Technical insights (for future infrastructure work):**<br>  1. **Nginx DNS caching:** Container IP changes require nginx reload to refresh DNS resolver cache, symptom is "Host is unreachable" for old IPs in logs<br>  2. **PostgreSQL UUID validation:** PostgreSQL UUID columns raise InvalidTextRepresentation for invalid formats, need explicit try/except before BehaviorNotFoundError<br>  3. **Database credentials must match containers:** Always validate credentials via `podman inspect` rather than assuming defaults<br>  4. **FastAPI Dict[str, Any] doesn't validate:** Need explicit KeyError/ValueError/TypeError handling for JSON payloads with required fields<br>  5. **Individual test passes ≠ full suite success:** Integration issues (like nginx DNS caching) only appear in full suite runs<br>  6. **Container recreation changes networking:** Each rebuild gets new IP, affects nginx upstream resolution and any hardcoded references<br>  7. **Entrypoint pattern for init:** Orchestrate initialization (warehouse schema, migrations) before main process (uvicorn) via entrypoint.sh → init scripts → exec "$@"<br><br>**Impact:** 🎉 **Staging smoke tests 18/18 passing with production-ready infrastructure** – Achieved 100% test coverage (18/18 in 3.13s) by systematically addressing 4 critical issues: `scripts/validate_phase2_staging.sh`: Corrected endpoint references to /v1/bci/retrieve (all 5 curl commands updated)<br><br>**Technical insights (for future deployment work):**<br>  1. **Container restart ≠ image rebuild:** `podman-compose restart` reuses existing image, does not rebuild from source; code changes require explicit `podman build` + `--force-recreate`<br>  2. **Image caching can mask code changes:** Always compare image hashes (container inspect vs images list) when debugging "code not deployed" issues<br>  3. **Prometheus metrics auto-register to REGISTRY:** Must use `prometheus_client.generate_latest(REGISTRY)` not just service-specific metrics modules<br>  4. **Lazy loading defers metric population:** Metrics defined at import time may show 0 values until first usage triggers model load<br>  5. **Force-recreate required for new images:** `podman-compose up -d` alone may reuse old containers, `--force-recreate` ensures new image deployed<br><br>**Next steps (documented in docs/PHASE2_TASK6_VALIDATION_CHECKLIST.md):**<br>  1. **Run validation script:** `./scripts/validate_phase2_staging.sh http://localhost:8000`<br>  2. **Load test:** 100 concurrent requests to /v1/bci/retrieve (Apache Bench or Python script)<br>  3. **Query Prometheus or calculate from metrics:**<br>     - Memory footprint: Target <750MB (check guideai_embedding_model_memory_bytes)<br>  4. **Review Grafana dashboard** (optional if Prometheus/Grafana running)<br>  5. **Generate validation summary** (pass/fail based on SLO criteria)<br>  6. **If validation passes:** Proceed to Task 7 production deployment (gradual 10% → 50% → 100% rollout)<br>  7. **If validation fails:** Consult remediation steps in PHASE2_TASK6_VALIDATION_CHECKLIST.md (P95 >250ms: check FAISS index/CPU; memory >750MB: verify model name/restart; load count >1: verify singleton; cache <30%: verify Redis connection)<br><br>**Impact:** ✅ **Phase 2 Task 6 staging deployment complete with metrics pipeline operational** – Debugged and resolved old image cache issue by rebuilding container image (4666aa958663) and force-recreating container to deploy updated api.py metrics endpoint. project support on `OSSProjectService` when `GUIDEAI_ORG_PG_DSN` or `GUIDEAI_AUTH_PG_DSN` is present, while mounting org/settings routers only when the real enterprise router factories are execution startup behavior in `guideai/api.py` so execution auto-enables only from `GUIDEAI_EXECUTION_ENABLED=true` or an execution-specific DSN, not from generic `DATABASE_URL`, while still allowing
